## Callbacks

These functions are called by the engine automatically:

| Callback | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `luna.load()` | Called once after the script is loaded |
| `luna.update(dt)` | Called every frame; `dt` is elapsed seconds |
| `luna.draw()` | Called every frame for rendering |
| `luna.keypressed(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is pressed |
| `luna.keyreleased(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is released |
| `luna.mousepressed(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is pressed |
| `luna.mousereleased(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is released |
| `luna.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch start |
| `luna.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch move |
| `luna.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch end |
| `luna.resize(w, h)` | Called when window is resized |
| `luna.focus(focused)` | Called when window gains/loses focus |
| `luna.quit()` | Called when the window is closed |
| `luna.gamepadpressed(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button press |
| `luna.gamepadreleased(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button release |
| `luna.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)` | Called on gamepad axis change |

#### `luna.graphics.captureScreenshot(callback)`

Captures the current frame as an `ImageData` and passes it to `callback`.

In headless or test mode this creates a blank transparent `ImageData` sized to the current window dimensions and calls `callback` synchronously. This remains a stub path used for headless and test environments.

**Parameters:**

- `callback` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `function`. Called with one `ImageData` argument.

**Returns:** Nothing.

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L4465)*

Queues draw commands for all live particles.

Lua API: luna.graphics.draw(image_id, x, y) Draws any drawable object Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Image, Canvas, or SpriteBatch Ă˘â‚¬â€ť at the given position. Backward-compatible: still accepts raw integer image IDs.

**Parameters:**

- `drawable` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `Drawable`. An Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch userdata, or integer image ID.

- `y` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Destination Y position (default 0).
- `r` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Rotation in radians (default 0).

#### `luna.graphics.drawEx(args)`

Draws any drawable object with a full affine transform.

Accepts Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch userdata or raw integer image IDs. When `sy` is omitted it defaults to `sx` for uniform scaling.

**Parameters:**

- `drawable` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `Drawable`. An Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch userdata or integer image ID.
- `x` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Destination X position.
- `y` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Destination Y position.
- `r` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Rotation in radians (default 0).
- `sx` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. X scale (default 1).
- `sy` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Y scale (default sx).
- `ox` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. X origin offset (default 0).
- `oy` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `f32`. Y origin offset (default 0).

**Returns:** `()`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L3937)*

#### `luna.graphics.saveScreenshot(path)`

Queues a PNG export of the actual rendered frame to a file under `save/`.

The path is validated immediately against the sandboxed `GameFS`, then written after the current frame finishes rendering through the normal GPU surface path.

**Parameters:**

- `path` â€” `string`. Relative output path inside `save/`, for example `"save/frame.png"`.

**Returns:** Nothing.

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L4439)*

### NineSlice Methods

#### `NineSlice:draw(x, y, w, h)`

Draws to the current render target.

**Parameters:**

- `x` Ä‚â€ťÄ‚â€ˇÄ‚Â¶ `number`.
- `y` Ä‚â€ťÄ‚â€ˇÄ‚Â¶ `number`.
- `w` Ä‚â€ťÄ‚â€ˇÄ‚Â¶ `number`.

## luna.window

Window Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for window api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

## luna.timer

Timer Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for timer api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*25 entries | 25 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.timer.getAverageDelta()`

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L371)*

@return any

@return any

#### `luna.math.simplexNoise(args)`

Standalone simplex noise: returns a value in approximately `[-1, 1]` for 1Ă˘â‚¬â€ś3 coordinates.

Equivalent to calling `luna.math.newNoiseGenerator(0):simplexNoise(...)`.

**Parameters:**

- `x` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť X coordinate.
- `y` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Y coordinate (optional, defaults to 0).
- `z` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Z coordinate (optional; enables 3-D mode).

**Returns:** Noise value in approximately `[-1.0, 1.0]`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L2371)*

### BezierCurve Methods

#### `BezierCurve:evaluate(t)`

Evaluates the curve at parameter t in [0, 1] and returns the world point.

**Parameters:**

- `t` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Curve parameter in the range [0, 1].

**Returns:** x, y coordinates of the point on the curve.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L259)*

---

#### `BezierCurve:getControlPoint(index)`

Returns the position of the control point at the given index.

**Parameters:**

- `i` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť 1-based index of the control point.

**Returns:** x, y coordinates of the control point.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L316)*

---

#### `BezierCurve:getControlPointCount()`

Returns the total number of control points in the curve.

**Returns:** Count of control points as an integer.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L380)*

---

#### `BezierCurve:getDerivative()`

Returns a new BezierCurve that is the derivative (degree reduced) of this curve.

**Returns:** New BezierCurve representing the tangent/derivative curve.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L301)*

---

#### `BezierCurve:removeControlPoint(index)`

Removes the control point at the given index from the curve.

**Parameters:**

- `i` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť 1-based index of the control point to remove.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L363)*

---

#### `BezierCurve:render([segments])`

Subdivides the curve to the given depth and returns the sample points.

**Parameters:**

- `depth` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Subdivision depth; higher values yield smoother output.

**Returns:** Flat list of (x, y) sample coordinates.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L271)*

---

#### `BezierCurve:translate(dx, dy)`

Shifts every control point by the given (dx, dy) offset in place.

**Parameters:**

- `dx` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Horizontal offset in pixels.
- `dy` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Vertical offset in pixels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L389)*

### Transform Methods

#### `Transform:clone()`

Returns an independent deep copy of this transform object.

**Returns:** A new Transform with identical matrix state.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L218)*

---

#### `Transform:getMatrix()`

Returns the 16 matrix elements of the 4x4 transform in column-major order.

**Returns:** 16 numbers representing the matrix elements.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L230)*

---

#### `Transform:inverse()`

Returns a new Transform that is the mathematical inverse of this one.

**Returns:** A new Transform whose matrix is the inverse.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L206)*

---

#### `Transform:inverseTransformPoint(x, y)`

Applies the inverse of this transform to the given point.

**Parameters:**

- `x` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Input X coordinate.
- `y` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Input Y coordinate.

**Returns:** Inverse-transformed x, y coordinates.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L197)*

---

#### `Transform:reset()`

Resets the internal matrix to the identity (no transform applied).

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L140)*

---

#### `Transform:rotate(angle)`

Applies a rotation by the given angle to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `angle` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Rotation angle in radians.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L113)*

---

#### `Transform:scale(sx, [sy])`

Applies a scale factor to the transform's internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `sx` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Horizontal scale factor.
- `sy` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Vertical scale factor (defaults to sx if omitted).

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L123)*

---

#### `Transform:shear(kx, ky)`

Applies a shear (skew) transformation to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `kx` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Horizontal shear factor.
- `ky` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Vertical shear factor.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L134)*

---

#### `Transform:transformPoint(x, y)`

Transforms a point (x, y) by this matrix and returns the result.

**Parameters:**

- `x` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Input X coordinate.
- `y` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Input Y coordinate.

**Returns:** Transformed x, y coordinates.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L184)*

---

#### `Transform:translate(dx, dy)`

Applies a translation offset to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `dx` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Horizontal offset in pixels.

## luna.audio

Audio Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for audio api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaSource`, `LuaBus`, `LuaMidiPlayer`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*164 entries | 159 documented*

## luna.filesystem

Filesystem Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for filesystem api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*37 entries | 37 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.filesystem.append(path, data)`

Opens the file in append mode and writes the given string at the end.

**Parameters:**

- `path` â€” Relative file path inside the save directory.
- `data` â€” String to append.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.
@param path : string
@param data : string

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L242)*

---

Status is "pending", "done", or "error". @param handle_id : integer @return any

### FileHandle Methods

#### `FileHandle:close()`

Flushes any pending writes and closes the file handle.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L144)*

---

#### `FileHandle:flush()`

Flushes all buffered writes to disk without closing the handle.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L133)*

---

#### `FileHandle:getMode()`

Returns the access mode the file was opened with.

@return any

**Returns:** One of 'r' (read), 'w' (write), or 'a' (append).

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L124)*

---

#### `FileHandle:getSize()`

Returns the size of the open file in bytes.

@return any

**Returns:** File size as an integer number of bytes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L114)*

---

#### `FileHandle:isEOF()`

Returns whether the read cursor has reached the end of the file.

**Returns:** true if at end-of-file, false otherwise.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L155)*

---

@param count : integer? @return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L47)*

---

#### `FileHandle:readLine()`

Reads the next line of text from the file and returns it as a string.

@return any

**Returns:** The line string (without newline), or nil at end of file.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L60)*

---

#### `FileHandle:seek(pos)`

Seeks the file position to the given byte offset from the start.

@param pos : integer @return any

**Parameters:**

- `offset` â€” Byte position to seek to (0-based).

**Returns:** The new byte position, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L88)*

---

#### `FileHandle:tell()`

---

#### `luna.event.restart()`

Requests that the engine restart at the beginning of the next frame.

Sets `SharedState::restart_requested` to `true`. The engine loop checks this flag after each frame and restarts if set.

**Returns:** `()`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L330)*

---

#### `luna.event.wait([timeout])`

Blocks until the next event arrives or the optional timeout elapses.

**Parameters:**

- `timeout` â€” `number?`. Timeout in seconds (optional; omit to wait indefinitely).

**Returns:** Event name and arguments, or nothing on timeout.

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L296)*

## luna.thread

Registers the `luna.thread` namespace.

Provides Lua-level multithreading: create background threads that run
independent Lua VMs and communicate via thread-safe channels.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for thread api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaThreadHandle`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

## luna.compute

Registers the `luna.compute.*` array computation API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for compute api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*43 entries | 43 documented*

### Functions

@param tbl : table @param shape : any? @param dtype : string?

**Parameters:** `tbl`, `shape`, `dtype`

## luna.dataframe

Registers the `luna.dataframe.*` tabular data API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for dataframe api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

## luna.data

Registers the `luna.data.*` LĂ–VE2D-compatible binary data API.

Provides the Lua-side `luna.data` namespace with functions that mirror the
LĂ–VE2D `love.data.*` surface: `pack`, `unpack`, `getPackedSize`,
`compress`, `decompress`, `encode`, `decode`, `hash`, `newByteData`,
and `newDataView`.

`luna.data.pack` / `luna.data.unpack` use the LĂ–VE2D format string
(`"<"` / `">"` prefix for endianness, single-char type codes such as `"b"`, `"H"`,
`"f"`, `"z"`, `"s"`, etc.) for byte-for-byte compatibility with LĂ–VE2D data files.
TOML round-trip helpers are also exposed here as `luna.data.parseToml` and
`luna.data.encodeToml`.
Luna2D Binary Pack Format (space-separated type tokens) is available via
`luna.data.write` / `luna.data.read` / `luna.data.size`.

*24 entries | 15 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.data.compress(format_str, raw_data, [level])`

Compresses data using the given algorithm (''deflate'', ''gzip'', ''lz4'').

@param format_str : string @param raw_data : string @param level : integer? @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `raw_data`, `level`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L95)*

---

#### `luna.data.decode(format_str, encoded)`

Decodes encoded text back to binary using the given format (''base64'', ''hex'').

@param format_str : string @param encoded : string @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `encoded`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L146)*

---

@param format_str : string @param compressed_data : string @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `compressed_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L114)*

---

#### `luna.data.pack(fmt, vals)`

Packs values into a binary byte string using the LĂ–VE2D format string.

The format prefix ``<`` / ``>`` selects little/big endian (default: little). Single-char type codes: b/B (int8/uint8), h/H (int16/uint16), i/I (int32/uint32), l/L (int64/uint64), f (float32), d (float64), z (null-terminated string), s (length-prefixed string), x (pad byte). @param format : string @return any

**Parameters:** `fmt`, `vals`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L43)*

---

#### `luna.data.parseToml(toml_string)`

Parses a TOML string and returns a Lua table representation.

@param toml_string : string @return any

**Parameters:** `toml_string`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L222)*

---

## luna.image

Registers the `luna.image.*` pixel-level image manipulation API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for image api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*8 entries | 6 documented*

### Functions

## luna.graph

Registers the `luna.graph.*` directed-graph and item-flow simulation API.

Exposes `LuaGraph`, `LuaNode`, `LuaEdge`, and `LuaGraphItem` UserData types
wrapping `crate::graph::Graph` with callback dispatch for simulation events.

*101 entries | 101 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.tilemap.hexArea(q, r, radius)`

Returns all hex cell coordinates within a given radius of center (q, r).

**Parameters:**

- `q` Ă”Ă‡Ă¶ Center q coordinate.
- `r` Ă”Ă‡Ă¶ Center r coordinate.
- `radius` Ă”Ă‡Ă¶ Radius in hex steps (1 = immediate ring, 2 = two rings, etc.).

**Returns:** Table of {q, r} coordinates for every cell within the radius.

*Source: [src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs](src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs#L2279)*

## luna.animation

Registers the `luna.animation` namespace.

Provides Lua-level sprite animation: frame pools, named clips, speed
control, and playback events.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the
implementation details for animation API-related operations.
Key types exported: `LuaAnimation`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

*13 entries | 13 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.animation.new()`

Creates a new, empty [`Animation`] controller.

@return Animation

*Source: [src/lua_api/animation_api.rs](src/lua_api/animation_api.rs#L235)*

#### `Animation:pollEvents()`

Drains and returns all pending animation events as a table.

## luna.automation

Automation Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

Registers the `luna.simulator.*` namespace for automated input simulation
via timed step scripts. Scripts inject synthetic input events into the
engine's event queue during playback.

## Exposed Lua API

| Function | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `luna.simulator.load(name, data)` | Load a script from a Lua step table |
| `luna.simulator.loadFromToml(name, toml_str)` | Load a script from a TOML string |
| `luna.simulator.loadFile(name, path)` | Load a script from a TOML file on disk |
| `luna.simulator.unload(name)` | Remove a loaded script by name |
| `luna.simulator.hasScript(name)` | Return `true` if a script is registered |
| `luna.simulator.getScripts()` | Return an array of all registered script names |
| `luna.simulator.start(name)` | Start playback from step zero |
| `luna.simulator.stop()` | Stop playback and reset to `Idle` |
| `luna.simulator.pause()` | Pause playback at the current position |
| `luna.simulator.resume()` | Resume from a paused position |
| `luna.simulator.update(dt)` | Advance the clock and dispatch due steps |
| `luna.simulator.isRunning()` | Return `true` if actively playing |
| `luna.simulator.isPaused()` | Return `true` if paused |
| `luna.simulator.isComplete()` | Return `true` if all steps dispatched |
| `luna.simulator.getCurrentStep()` | Return the index of the next step |
| `luna.simulator.getStepCount()` | Return the total step count |
| `luna.simulator.getCurrentScript()` | Return the active script name or `nil` |
| `luna.simulator.getElapsedTime()` | Return seconds elapsed since `start` |

## Implementation Pattern

A single `Rc<RefCell<Simulator>>` is created at registration time and
captured by all closures via Rc clone. The `SharedState` borrow is held
only long enough to push events â€” never across yield points.

*16 entries | 0 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.automation.getCurrentScript()`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L286)*

## luna.camera

Registers the `luna.camera` namespace.

Provides Lua-level camera management: smooth follow, dead zone,
screen-shake, bounds clamping, and coordinate conversion via [`Camera2D`].

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem.
Key types exported: `LuaCamera2D`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

*23 entries | 23 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.camera.new(vw, vh)`

@param viewport_w number @param viewport_h number @return Camera2D

**Parameters:** `vw`, `vh`

*Source: [src/lua_api/camera_api.rs](src/lua_api/camera_api.rs#L241)*

## luna.debugbridge

Registers the `luna.debugbridge.*` TCP debug server API.

Embeds a JSON-over-TCP server (127.0.0.1 only) inside the running game.
External tools (VS Code extension, MCP server) connect to inspect and
control the game at runtime. Network I/O runs on a background thread;
Lua-dependent methods are queued and dispatched via `poll()` on the main thread.

*15 entries | 15 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.debugbridge.broadcast(event, json_data)`

Broadcasts a JSON event to all connected clients.

@param event : string @param json_data : string

**Parameters:** `event`, `json_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L794)*

---

**Parameters:** `msg`, `source`, `line`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L620)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.clearPrintHistory()`

Clears the print history.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L689)*

## luna.entity

Registers the `luna.entity.*` ECS universe API.

Exposes `Universe` as Lua UserData (`LuaUniverse`) with entity lifecycle,
component operations, querying, systems, tags, layers, and blueprints.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for entity api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*43 entries | 43 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.entity.newUniverse()`

New universe.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/entity_api.rs](src/lua_api/entity_api.rs#L648)*

## luna.font

Lua API bindings for the `luna.font.*` font rasterizer module.

Provides `newRasterizer`, `newTrueTypeRasterizer`, `newBMFontRasterizer`,
and `newGlyphData` factory functions matching the LĂ–VE2D `love.font` module
surface.  Font loading delegates to the same `Font::from_bytes` path used by
`luna.graphics.newFont` so the returned `LuaFont` userdata is fully
compatible with all existing graphics API functions.

*11 entries | 11 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.font.newBMFontRasterizer(image_file, glyph_hints)`

Stub: BMFont rasterization is not yet supported.

Raises a descriptive Lua error so scripts fail fast with a clear message rather than a cryptic nil-dereference.

**Parameters:** `image_file`, `glyph_hints`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L199)*

---

#### `luna.font.newGlyphData(font_val, codepoint)`

Returns glyph metrics for a given Unicode code point within the font.

`font` may be a `LuaFont` userdata or a raw font ID integer. `codepoint` is a Unicode integer (e.g. `string.byte("A")` = 65).

**Parameters:** `font_val`, `codepoint`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L216)*

---

#### `luna.font.newRasterizer(path, [size])`

Loads a TTF/OTF font file and returns a font userdata object.

This is an alias for `luna.graphics.newFont` exposed on the `luna.font` module for LĂ–VE2D compatibility.

**Parameters:** `path`, `size`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L172)*

---

#### `luna.font.newTrueTypeRasterizer(path, [size], [hinting])`

Loads a TTF/OTF font with an optional hinting hint (currently ignored).

The `hinting` parameter is accepted for API compatibility but has no effect â€” fontdue uses its own hinting strategy internally.

**Parameters:** `path`, `size`, `hinting`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L185)*

---

### GlyphData Methods

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L78)*

#### `GlyphData:getGlyphString()`

Returns the glyph character as a UTF-8 string.

**Returns:** `string`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L102)*

**Returns:** `integer`

## luna.gui

Lua API bindings for the `luna.gui.*` retained-mode widget system.

Registers the `luna.gui` namespace with functions for creating widgets,
managing the widget tree, routing input events, theming, focus navigation,
and toast notifications.

## Exposed Lua API

| Function | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `luna.gui.newButton(text?)` | Create a button widget |
| `luna.gui.newLabel(text?)` | Create a text label |
| `luna.gui.newTextInput()` | Create a text input field |
| `luna.gui.newCheckbox(text?)` | Create a checkbox |
| `luna.gui.newSlider(min?, max?)` | Create a value slider |
| `luna.gui.newProgressBar(min?, max?)` | Create a progress bar |
| `luna.gui.newComboBox()` | Create a dropdown |
| `luna.gui.newList()` | Create a selectable list |
| `luna.gui.newPanel()` | Create a container panel |
| `luna.gui.newLayout(direction?)` | Create a flexbox layout |
| `luna.gui.newScrollPanel()` | Create a scrollable panel |
| `luna.gui.newNinePatch()` | Create a 9-patch slicer |
| `luna.gui.newTabBar()` | Create a tab bar |
| `luna.gui.newSeparator(vertical?)` | Create a separator line |
| `luna.gui.newSpacer(w?, h?)` | Create spacing filler |
| `luna.gui.newToast(msg?, duration?)` | Create a toast notification |
| `luna.gui.newTreeView()` | Create a collapsible tree |
| `luna.gui.newRadioButton(text?, group?)` | Create a grouped radio button |
| `luna.gui.newScrollBar(vertical?)` | Create a scroll bar |
| `luna.gui.newWindow(title?)` | Create a draggable window |
| `luna.gui.newSplitPanel(orientation?)` | Create a split panel |
| `luna.gui.newDockPanel()` | Create a dock panel |
| `luna.gui.newToolbar(orientation?)` | Create a toolbar |
| `luna.gui.newMenuBar()` | Create a menu bar |
| `luna.gui.newMenuItem(text?)` | Create a menu item |
| `luna.gui.newDialog(title?)` | Create a modal dialog |
| `luna.gui.newStatusBar()` | Create a status bar |
| `luna.gui.newAccordion()` | Create a collapsible accordion |
| `luna.gui.newTooltipPanel(text?)` | Create a tooltip panel |
| `luna.gui.newColorPicker()` | Create a color picker |
| `luna.gui.newTable()` | Create a data table |
| `luna.gui.newImageWidget()` | Create an image widget |
| `luna.gui.newTheme()` | Create a theme instance |
| `luna.gui.setTheme(theme)` | Set the active theme |
| `luna.gui.getTheme()` | Get the active theme |
| `luna.gui.getRoot()` | Get the root panel index |
| `luna.gui.setFocus(idx/nil)` | Set keyboard focus |
| `luna.gui.getFocus()` | Get focused widget index |
| `luna.gui.focusNext()` | Tab to next focusable |
| `luna.gui.focusPrev()` | Tab to previous focusable |
| `luna.gui.clearFocus()` | Clear focus |
| `luna.gui.addToast(toast)` | Queue a toast overlay |
| `luna.gui.getToastCount()` | Active toast count |
| `luna.gui.mousepressed(x,y,btn?)` | Forward mouse press |
| `luna.gui.mousereleased(x,y,btn?)` | Forward mouse release |
| `luna.gui.mousemoved(x,y)` | Forward mouse move |
| `luna.gui.keypressed(key)` | Forward key press |
| `luna.gui.textinput(text)` | Forward text input |
| `luna.gui.wheelmoved(x,y)` | Forward mouse wheel |
| `luna.gui.update(dt)` | Advance toast timers |
| `luna.gui.getWidgetCount()` | Total widget count |
| Widget methods | See per-type method tables in `src/gui/AGENT.md` |

## Implementation Pattern

A single `Rc<RefCell<GuiContext>>` is created at registration time and
captured by all closures via Rc clone.  Widget indices (pool positions)
are returned to Lua as integers.  Container/list/tab indices are 1-based
in Lua.

*314 entries | 276 documented*

## luna.light

Registers the `luna.light.*` 2D lighting API.

Provides Lua bindings for creating and managing 2D point lights
and polygon shadow occluders via the `LightWorld` resource pool.

*74 entries | 0 documented*

## luna.localization

Registers the `luna.localization.*` internationalization API.

Provides a structured translation system supporting multiple languages,
fallback chains, pluralization, variable interpolation, and language-change
callbacks.

## luna.log

Structured game-level logging API (`luna.log.*`).

Exposes convenience logging functions so Lua scripts can emit messages at
specific severity levels and query or change the active log level at
runtime without going through the `luna.system` namespace.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.log.debug(message)`

Emit a debug-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` â€” The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L31)*

---

#### `luna.log.error(message)`

Emit an error-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` â€” The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L73)*

---

#### `luna.log.getLevel()`

Return the name of the currently active minimum log level.

**Returns:** One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L127)*

---

#### `luna.log.info(message)`

Emit an info-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` â€” The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L45)*

---

#### `luna.log.print(level, message)`

Emit a log message from Lua at the specified severity level.

@param level : string @param message : string

Accepts the same level strings as `luna.log.setLevel`: `"debug"`, `"info"`, `"warn"`, `"error"`, `"trace"`. Unknown levels fall back to `info`.

**Parameters:**

- `level` â€” Severity level string.
- `message` â€” The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L93)*

---

#### `luna.log.setLevel(level)`

Set the minimum severity level for runtime log messages.

@param level : string

**Parameters:**

- `level` â€” One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L114)*

---

#### `luna.log.warn(message)`

Emit a warn-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` â€” The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L59)*

## luna.minimap

Lua API bindings for the `luna.minimap.*` minimap module.

Provides a `Minimap` UserData type with factory functions for creating
grid-based minimaps with terrain coloring, fog of war, tracked objects,
pings, markers, and viewport rectangle overlay.

*49 entries | 47 documented*

## luna.network

Registers the `luna.network` namespace.

Provides Lua-level UDP networking via ENet: host creation, peer
management, packet sending and receiving. Wraps [`NetworkHost`].

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem.
Key types exported: `LuaNetworkHost`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

*5 entries | 5 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.network.newHost(opts)`

Creates a new [`NetworkHost`] bound to the given address.

`opts` fields: - `addr`     â€” `string`  Bind address `"host:port"`. Use `"0.0.0.0:0"` for a client-only host. - `peers`    â€” `number`  Maximum number of peers (default 32). - `channels` â€” `number`  Channel count (default 2). @param opts table @return NetworkHost

**Parameters:** `opts`

*Source: [src/lua_api/network_api.rs](src/lua_api/network_api.rs#L215)*

---

### NetworkHost Methods

#### `NetworkHost:disconnect(peer_id_raw, [data])`

Gracefully disconnects a peer. The disconnect event arrives on the next `service()`.

@param peer_id number @param data    number  (default 0) User data for the disconnect packet.

**Parameters:** `peer_id_raw`, `data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/network_api.rs](src/lua_api/network_api.rs#L178)*

---

#### `NetworkHost:flush()`

Flushes pending sends immediately.

*Source: [src/lua_api/network_api.rs](src/lua_api/network_api.rs#L168)*

---

#### `NetworkHost:getAddress()`

Returns the local address of this host as `"ip:port"`.

@return string

*Source: [src/lua_api/network_api.rs](src/lua_api/network_api.rs#L188)*

---

#### `NetworkHost:service()`

Polls the network for one event. Returns an event table or `nil`.

Event table: `{type, peer_id [, channel_id] [, data]}`. `type` is `"connect"`, `"disconnect"`, or `"receive"`. @return table|nil

*Source: [src/lua_api/network_api.rs](src/lua_api/network_api.rs#L84)*

---


## luna.overlay

Registers the `luna.overlay` table and exposes a single factory:

- `luna.overlay.newOverlay(width?, height?)` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť creates a `LuaOverlay`
  UserData object.

All overlay state lives entirely inside an `Rc<RefCell<Overlay>>`; the
`LuaOverlay` wrapper holds a clone of that smart pointer. Calling any
method borrows the `RefCell` for the duration of the call, then
releases it Ă˘â‚¬â€ť the engine never holds a long-lived `borrow_mut` across
Lua callbacks.

The `register` function is called once during engine startup by the
`lua_api` module registration chain; it adds the `luna.overlay` table
to the root `luna` global.

*57 entries | 56 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.overlay.newOverlay([width], [height])`

*(undocumented)*

**Parameters:** `width`, `height`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L732)*

---

### Overlay Methods

#### `Overlay:clear()`

Resets all overlay subsystems to their inactive defaults.

Equivalent to calling `Overlay::clear()` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť drops all live weather particles, deactivates flash/shake/fade/lightning, and disables ambient, clouds, fog, heat haze, vignette, and film grain. All parameters (intensity, colour, duration) are reset to their initial values. Useful when transitioning between scenes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L122)*

---

#### `Overlay:draw()`

Placeholder for draw Ă˘â‚¬â€ť actual rendering handled by the game loop.

#### `Overlay:resize(w, h)`

Updates the internal canvas dimensions on window resize.

Informs the weather particle spawner of the new screen bounds so that particles are culled and spawned correctly after a window resize event. Does not drop existing particles. @param width : number @param height : number

**Parameters:** `w`, `h`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L81)*

---

#### `Overlay:setAmbientEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables automatic time-of-day ambient colour cycling.

When `true`, `update()` calls `compute_color_from_time()` each frame and overwrites `ambient.color`. When `false`, the colour set via `setAmbientColor` is used as a static tint. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L195)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudCount(count)`

Sets the number of cloud shadow blobs rendered each frame.

Higher counts produce denser, more uniform coverage. Each blob is positioned pseudo-randomly based on its index, so the layout is consistent across frames. @param count : number

**Parameters:** `count`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L439)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudOpacity(opacity)`

Sets the cloud shadow overlay opacity (0.0 = invisible, 1.0 = fully dark).

Controls how darkly the shadow blobs are blended over the scene. 0.3 gives a subtle day-time look; 0.7Ă˘â‚¬â€ś0.9 simulates heavy overcast. @param opacity : number

**Parameters:** `opacity`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L487)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudScale(scale)`

Sets the relative size scale of each cloud shadow blob.

1.0 is the default blob size; smaller values produce compact dappled shadows; larger values produce wide overcast patches. @param scale : number

**Parameters:** `scale`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L471)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudShadows(enabled)`

Enables or disables the scrolling cloud shadow overlay.

Cloud shadows are rendered as soft blob-shaped shadow blobs drifting horizontally across the scene. Configure their appearance with `setCloudCount`, `setCloudScale`, and `setCloudOpacity`. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L422)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudSpeed(speed)`

Sets the horizontal scroll speed of cloud shadows in pixels per second.

The internal `offset` accumulator grows without bound; the renderer wraps it modulo screen width so shadows loop seamlessly. @param speed : number

**Parameters:** `speed`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L455)*

---

#### `Overlay:setFilmGrainEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables per-frame random film grain noise.

The noise pattern is regenerated every frame so it does not repeat or create a visible flicker texture. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L644)*

---

#### `Overlay:setFilmGrainIntensity(intensity)`

Sets the film grain noise amplitude (0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś1.0).

0.1Ă˘â‚¬â€ś0.3 gives a subtle cinematic look. Values above 0.5 produce heavy grain that can obscure fine detail. @param intensity : number

**Parameters:** `intensity`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L660)*

---

#### `Overlay:setFogDensity(density)`

Sets the fog density (0.0 = invisible, 1.0 = fully opaque).

Maps directly to the alpha of the fog colour overlay. @param density : number

**Parameters:** `density`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L525)*

---

#### `Overlay:setFogEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables atmospheric fog.

@param enabled : boolean Enables or disables the atmospheric fog overlay.

When enabled, a translucent colour rectangle is blended over the full scene every frame. Configure thickness via `setFogDensity` and colour via `setFogColor`.

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L510)*

---

#### `Overlay:setHeatHazeEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables UV-distortion heat shimmer.

When enabled, the renderer applies a time-animated sine wave displacement to the scene's UV coordinates, simulating the wavering distortion seen above hot surfaces. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L570)*

---

#### `Overlay:setHeatHazeIntensity(intensity)`

Sets the heat haze distortion intensity.

Controls the peak UV displacement in pixels. 0.2Ă˘â‚¬â€ś2.0 gives subtle mirage shimmer; higher values are suitable for extreme heat or magical warp effects. @param intensity : number

**Parameters:** `intensity`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L587)*

---

#### `Overlay:setTimeOfDay(hour)`

Sets the time-of-day value that drives ambient colour cycling.

The value is in 24-hour floating-point format (0.0 = midnight, 12.0 = noon, 24.0 wraps to midnight again). Has no visible effect unless ambient cycling is enabled via `setAmbientEnabled`. @param hour : number

**Parameters:** `hour`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L178)*

---

#### `Overlay:setVignetteEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables screen-edge darkening (vignette).

The vignette grades from transparent at the screen centre to near-black at the corners. Useful for suggesting restricted vision, dramatic tension, or a cinematic look. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L608)*

---

#### `Overlay:setVignetteStrength(strength)`

Sets the vignette darkening strength (0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś1.0).

0.0 is invisible; 0.5 is a gentle filmic border; 1.0 crushes corners to near-black. @param strength : number

**Parameters:** `strength`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L624)*

---

#### `Overlay:setWeather(name)`

Sets the active weather type by name.

Valid names: `"none"`, `"rain"`, `"snow"`, `"hail"`, `"dust"`, `"leaves"`, `"ash"`, `"pollen"`. The new type takes effect on the next `update` call Ă˘â‚¬â€ť existing particles are not cleared, so there may be a brief mix of old and new particle behaviors. Returns a Lua error if `name` is unrecognised. @param weather_type : string

**Parameters:** `name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L218)*

---

#### `Overlay:setWeatherEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables the weather particle spawner.

When disabled, no new particles are spawned but existing ones continue to move and age until they leave the screen. Set the weather type to `"none"` first if you want an immediate cutoff. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L291)*

---

#### `Overlay:setWeatherIntensity(intensity)`

Sets the weather particle density.

Controls both the maximum particle count (up to 200) and the spawn rate. 0.0 stops spawning; 1.0 produces the maximum particle density for the current weather type. @param intensity : number

**Parameters:** `intensity`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L241)*

---

#### `Overlay:setWindDirection(angle)`

Sets the wind direction as an angle in radians.

0.0 blows particles to the right; `math.pi / 2` blows downward. Combined with `setWindSpeed`, this drifts all live particles each frame by the wind velocity vector. @param angle : number

**Parameters:** `angle`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L258)*

---

#### `Overlay:setWindSpeed(speed)`

Sets the wind speed in pixels per second.

Adds a global velocity offset to every live weather particle each frame. 0.0 disables wind drift. @param speed : number

**Parameters:** `speed`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L274)*

---

#### `Overlay:triggerLightning()`

Triggers a one-shot lightning flash.

Fires a brief hard white flash (default 0.15 s). Calling while a flash is in progress restarts it from full brightness. Customise the flash colour first with `setLightningColor`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L680)*

---

#### `Overlay:update(dt)`

Advances all active overlay subsystems by `dt` seconds.

Drives weather particle spawning and culling, flash and shake decay, fade interpolation, cloud scroll accumulation, and lightning deactivation. Call exactly once per frame in `luna.update(dt)` before reading any derived state such as `getShakeOffset` or `isFlashing`. @param dt : number

**Parameters:** `dt`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L66)*

---


## luna.pathfinding

Registers the `luna.pathfinding.*` grid-based pathfinding API.

Exposes `NavGrid`, `UnitPathfinder`, and `FlowField` as Lua UserData
with 1-based tile coordinates at the Lua boundary.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for pathfinding api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*50 entries | 36 documented*

## luna.patterns

Registers the `luna.patterns.*` software design patterns API.

Provides factory functions and UserData wrappers for reusable patterns:
EventBus (prioritized pub-sub), ObjectPool (object reuse), CommandStack
(undo/redo), ServiceLocator (DI container), Factory (named constructors),
and SimpleState (finite state machine).

*47 entries | 47 documented*

## luna.pipeline

Registers the `luna.pipeline.*` DAG pipeline orchestrator API.

Exposes `LuaStep` and `LuaPipeline` UserData types wrapping `crate::pipeline`
with Lua callback dispatch for step execution.

Primary entry point: `register()`.

## luna.postfx

Registers the `luna.postfx` table and exposes factory functions:

- `luna.postfx.newEffect(name)` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť creates a built-in `PostFxEffect`
  by name (`"bloom"`, `"blur"`, `"crt"`, `"godrays"`, `"vignette"`,
  `"colourgrade"`, `"chromatic"`).
- `luna.postfx.newPass(shaderId)` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť creates a `Custom` `PostFxEffect`
  backed by an external shader resource ID.
- `luna.postfx.newStack(width?, height?)` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť creates an empty
  `PostFxStack` with the given canvas dimensions.
- `luna.postfx.newImageEffect(...)` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť creates a per-image
  [`LuaImageEffect`] chain (empty, single-effect, chain-table, or
  options-table overloads).
- `luna.postfx.loadImageEffect(path)` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť loads a [`LuaImageEffect`]
  chain from a TOML preset file.

`LuaPostFxEffect`, `LuaPostFxStack`, and `LuaImageEffect` are thin
`mlua` UserData wrappers that hold `Rc<RefCell<...>>` smart pointers.
`LuaPostFxStack` additionally owns the concrete effect vector so that
effect objects added via Lua are kept alive as long as the stack is alive.
`LuaImageEffect` stores [`crate::fx::post::PostFxEffect`] values directly
inside its [`crate::fx::post::ImageEffect`] and is passed to
`luna.graphics.draw` via the `effect` key of the options-table overload.

The `register` function is called once during engine startup.

*44 entries | 43 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.postfx.getEffectTypes()`

Returns a Lua table listing all valid built-in effect type names.

Useful for introspection tools or mod loaders that enumerate available effects without hard-coding the list. @return table<string>

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L967)*

---

#### `luna.postfx.loadImageEffect(path)`

Loads a per-image effect chain from a TOML preset file saved by `ImageEffect:save`.

@param path : string @return ImageEffect

**Parameters:** `path`

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L1096)*

---

#### `luna.postfx.newEffect(name)`

Creates a built-in post-processing effect by name.

Valid names: `"bloom"`, `"blur"`, `"crt"`, `"godrays"`, `"vignette"`, `"colourgrade"`, `"chromatic"`. Returns an error if the name is not recognised. Default parameters are populated automatically; call `setParameter` to override them. @param name : string @return PostFxEffect

**Parameters:** `name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L895)*

---

#### `luna.postfx.newImageEffect(args)`

Creates a per-image effect chain.

Overloads: - `newImageEffect()` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť empty chain. - `newImageEffect("blur")` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť chain with a single named effect. - `newImageEffect("blur", {radius=4})` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť single effect with initial parameters. - `newImageEffect({{type="blur",radius=2},{type="sepia"}})` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť chain from an array of spec tables. @return ImageEffect

**Parameters:** `args`

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L1005)*

---

#### `luna.postfx.newPass(shader_id)`

Creates a custom shader pass effect.

The returned `PostFxEffect` has `effect_type = Custom` and starts with an empty parameter map. The `shader_id` is passed to the GPU layer during `apply()` so it can look up and dispatch the correct user-supplied shader. @param shader_id : integer @return PostFxEffect

**Parameters:** `shader_id`

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L920)*

---

#### `luna.postfx.newStack([w], [h])`

*(undocumented)*

**Parameters:** `w`, `h`

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L942)*

---

### ImageEffect Methods

#### `ImageEffect:addEffect(name)`

Appends a new effect pass by name to the end of this effect chain.

Creates the effect internally and returns a shared handle so that parameter mutations through the returned object are visible in the chain.

**Parameters:**

- `name` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `string` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Effect type name (e.g. `"blur"`, `"sepia"`).

**Returns:** `PostFxEffect` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Shared handle to the newly added effect.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L734)*

---

#### `ImageEffect:clearEffects()`

Removes all effects from this chain.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L798)*

---

#### `ImageEffect:clone()`

Returns a deep clone of this `ImageEffect`.

The returned object shares no state with the original.

**Returns:** `ImageEffect`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L809)*

---

#### `ImageEffect:effectCount()`

Returns the number of effects in this chain.

**Returns:** `integer`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L773)*

---

#### `ImageEffect:getEffect(key)`

Returns the effect at the given 1-based index or by name, or `nil`.

When the first argument is an integer, retrieves by 1-based position. When it is a string, retrieves the first effect whose type name matches.

**Parameters:**

- `key` ? `integer | string` ? 1-based index or effect type name.

**Returns:** `PostFxEffect | nil`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L756)*

---

#### `ImageEffect:removeEffect(key)`

Removes an effect by 1-based index or by type name.

**Parameters:**

- `key` ? `integer | string` ? 1-based index or effect type name.

**Returns:** `boolean` ? `true` if the effect was found and removed.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L784)*

---

#### `ImageEffect:save(path)`

Serialises this effect chain to a TOML file at the given path.

**Parameters:**

- `path` ? `string` ? Destination file path.

**Returns:** `()`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L827)*

### PostFxEffect Methods

#### `PostFxEffect:getEffectType()`

Returns the string name of this effect's type.

Alias for `getType`. Provided for API consistency Ă˘â‚¬â€ť both names return the same value.

**Returns:** `string` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Effect type name.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L154)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:getParameterNames()`

Returns a sorted list of all parameter names currently set on this effect.

The returned Lua table is 1-indexed and sorted alphabetically. Useful for iterating all parameters during serialisation or building a parameter UI.

**Returns:** `table<string>` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Sorted array of parameter name strings.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L124)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:getType()`

Returns the string name of this effect's type.

Corresponds to `PostFxEffectType::name()`. Returns `"custom"` for custom shader pass effects created with `newPass`.

**Returns:** `string` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť One of `"bloom"`, `"blur"`, `"crt"`, `"godrays"`,
`"vignette"`, `"colourgrade"`, `"chromatic"`, or `"custom"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L142)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:hasParameter(name)`

Returns `true` if the named parameter exists on this effect.

Useful for introspection and serialisation. Custom effects start with an empty parameter map, so this will return `false` for any name until `setParameter` is called.

**Parameters:**

- `name` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `string` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Parameter key to test.

**Returns:** `boolean` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `true` if the key is present in the params map.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L111)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:isBuiltIn()`

Returns `true` if this is a built-in effect (not a custom shader pass).

Returns `false` for effects created with `luna.postfx.newPass`.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L165)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:isEnabled()`

Returns `true` if this effect is currently enabled.

Disabled effects are skipped by the stack during `apply()` without being removed from the chain. Enable/disable state can be toggled at any time without affecting the effect's parameters.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L178)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setBrightness(value)`

Sets the colour grading brightness multiplier.

Applied as a uniform scale across all channels before contrast and saturation adjustments. 1.0 is neutral; values below 1.0 darken the scene; values above 1.0 brighten it.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Brightness multiplier (default 1.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L319)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setContrast(value)`

Sets the colour grading contrast.

Pivots around mid-grey (0.5). Values above 1.0 push darks darker and lights lighter; values below 1.0 flatten the tonal range.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Contrast multiplier (default 1.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L338)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables this effect within its parent stack.

When disabled the effect remains in the chain at its current position but is skipped during `apply()`. Re-enabling it restores the pass at the same position.

**Parameters:**

- `enabled` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `boolean` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `true` to activate, `false` to skip.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L189)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setIntensity(value)`

Sets the intensity for bloom or godrays effects.

For bloom: scales the brightness of the blurred highlight layer before it is composited back onto the scene. For godrays: controls the overall brightness of the light ray overlay.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Intensity multiplier (typically 0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś2.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L225)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setOffset(value)`

Sets the chromatic aberration pixel offset.

The R, G, and B channels are sampled at offsets proportional to this value. Larger values produce a more extreme colour-fringing effect. Typical range is 1Ă˘â‚¬â€ś5 pixels.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Pixel offset for channel separation.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L299)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setParameter(name, value)`

Sets a named float parameter on the effect.

Inserts or replaces the parameter keyed by `name`. Common parameter names per effect type: `"threshold"` and `"intensity"` for bloom; `"radius"` and `"strength"` for blur; `"scanline_strength"` for CRT; `"offset"` for chromatic; `"strength"` for vignette; `"brightness"`, `"contrast"`, `"saturation"` for colour grading.

**Parameters:**

- `name` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `string` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Parameter key.
- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť New float value.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L77)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setRadius(value)`

Sets the Gaussian blur radius.

Larger values spread the blur sample footprint across more pixels. Values above ~8 may be expensive on integrated GPUs.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Blur radius in pixels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L260)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setSaturation(value)`

Sets the colour grading saturation.

0.0 produces a greyscale image; 1.0 is neutral; values above 1.0 boost colour vividness. Applied after brightness and contrast.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Saturation multiplier (0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś2.0, default 1.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L357)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setScanlineStrength(value)`

Sets the CRT scanline strength.

Controls how prominent the dark horizontal scanlines are in the CRT monitor simulation. 0.0 disables the scanline overlay; 1.0 produces fully black lines every other row.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Scanline opacity (0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś1.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L245)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setStrength(value)`

Sets the vignette or blur strength.

For vignette: 0.0 is invisible; 1.0 darkens the corners to black. For blur: scales the overall blur weight applied per sample.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Strength factor (0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś1.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L279)*

---

#### `PostFxEffect:setThreshold(value)`

Sets the bloom bright-pass threshold.

Pixels with luminance above this threshold contribute to the bloom effect. Typical values are 0.5Ă˘â‚¬â€ś0.9; lower values bleed bloom onto more of the scene.

**Parameters:**

- `value` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `number` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Threshold luminance (0.0Ă˘â‚¬â€ś1.0).

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L205)*

---

### PostFxStack Methods

#### `PostFxStack:add(effect)`

Appends a `PostFxEffect` to the end of the stack.

Effects are applied in insertion order during `apply()`. The effect is registered in the local effects registry and its index is appended to the `PostFxStack` chain. The effect is enabled by default.

**Parameters:**

- `effect` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `PostFxEffect` userdata Ă˘â‚¬â€ť The effect to append.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L409)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:apply()`

Applies all enabled effects in the stack.

Composites the captured image through each enabled effect in chain order and blends the result onto the current render target. Call this after `endCapture()` in `luna.draw`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L687)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:beginCapture()`

Starts a post-processing capture pass.

All `luna.graphics.*` draw calls between `beginCapture` and `endCapture` will target the post-FX canvas instead of the screen. Pair with `endCapture()` and `apply()` to see the effects. Returns an error if a capture is already in progress.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L652)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:endCapture()`

Ends a post-processing capture pass.

Must be called after `beginCapture()`. After this returns the engine resumes drawing to the normal screen target. Call `apply()` afterwards to composite the captured frame through the effect chain.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L672)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:getDimensions()`

Returns both canvas dimensions as `(width, height)`.

**Returns:** `integer, integer` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Width and height in pixels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L629)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:getEffect(index)`

Returns the effect at a 1-based position in the chain, or `nil`.

Provides random access into the chain. Returns the `LuaPostFxEffect` UserData at that position, or `nil` if `index` is out of range. The returned object is shared Ă˘â‚¬â€ť mutations to it are visible immediately through any other Lua variable holding the same effect.

**Parameters:**

- `index` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `integer` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť 1-based position in the chain.

**Returns:** `PostFxEffect | nil`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L551)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:getEffectCount()`

Returns the number of effects currently in the chain (enabled and disabled).

Useful for iterating via `getEffect(i)` from Lua.

**Returns:** `integer` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Total effects in the chain.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L533)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:getEnabledEffects()`

Returns a Lua table of all currently enabled effects in application order.

Used by the GPU layer during `apply()` to determine which shader passes to run. Disabled effects are excluded. The returned table is 1-indexed and contains `PostFxEffect` UserData objects.

**Returns:** `table<PostFxEffect>` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť Enabled effects in chain order.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L573)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:getHeight()`

Returns the canvas height in pixels.

**Returns:** `integer`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L620)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:getWidth()`

Returns the canvas width in pixels.

**Returns:** `integer`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L611)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:isCapturing()`

Returns `true` while the stack is between `beginCapture` and `endCapture`.

Useful for guard checks in Lua to avoid nested capture calls.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L640)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:isEffectEnabled(effect)`

Returns `true` if the given effect is enabled within this stack.

Queries the per-position enabled flag in the chain. Returns `false` if the effect is not in this stack's registry at all. This is distinct from `effect:isEnabled()`, which reads the enabled flag stored directly on the `PostFxEffect` object; both flags must be `true` for the pass to execute during `apply()`.

**Parameters:**

- `effect` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `PostFxEffect` userdata Ă˘â‚¬â€ť The effect to query.

**Returns:** `boolean` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `false` if the effect is absent from the chain.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L514)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:remove(effect)`

Removes a `PostFxEffect` from the stack chain.

Identifies the effect by pointer equality against the local registry. After removal all subsequent effects shift down by one position. Returns `false` if the effect is not in this stack's registry.

**Parameters:**

- `effect` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `PostFxEffect` userdata Ă˘â‚¬â€ť The effect to remove.

**Returns:** `boolean` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `true` if the effect was found and removed.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L433)*

---

#### `PostFxStack:resize(w, h)`

Resizes the internal canvas dimensions.

Call this whenever the window or render target changes size so the GPU layer can recreate ping-pong canvases at the correct resolution. Does not remove or invalidate any effects in the chain.

**Parameters:**

- `w` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `integer` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť New canvas width in pixels.
- `h` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť `integer` Ă˘â‚¬â€ť New canvas height in pixels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs](src/lua_api/postfx_api.rs#L601)*

---


## luna.procgen

Registers the `luna.procgen` namespace.

Exposes stateless procedural generation utilities: cellular-automata
cave maps, BFS flood fill, Poisson disk sampling, periodic Perlin noise,
and Voronoi diagrams.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem.
Primary functions: `register()`.

*5 entries | 5 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.procgen.cellularAutomata(w, h, [opts])`

Generates a cave-like map using cellular automata.

`opts` fields (all optional): - `fill`       â€” `number`  Initial fill probability 0â€“1 (default 0.45). - `iterations` â€” `number`  Smoothing iterations (default 5). - `birth`      â€” `number`  Live-cell birth threshold (default 4). - `survive`    â€” `number`  Live-cell survival threshold (default 3). - `seed`       â€” `number`  Random seed (default 0). Returns a flat Lua table of `w * h` bytes (0 = empty, 1 = wall). @param w    number  Grid width. @param h    number  Grid height. @param opts table   (optional) @return table

**Parameters:** `w`, `h`, `opts`

*Source: [src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs](src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs#L46)*

---

#### `luna.procgen.floodFill`

BFS flood fill on a flat grid of bytes.

Returns a flat Lua table (same size as `data`) with 1 for filled cells and 0 for unfilled cells. @param data      table   Flat grid of byte values (1-based). @param w         number  Grid width. @param h         number  Grid height. @param sx        number  Seed column (0-based). @param sy        number  Seed row    (0-based). @param threshold number  Fill boundary value (default 128). @param above     boolean If true fill cells >= threshold; else <= threshold (default false). @return table

*Source: [src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs](src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs#L81)*

---

#### `luna.procgen.perlinNoise(x, y, px, py)`

Evaluates a single periodic Perlin noise value at `(x, y)`.

`px` and `py` are the tile periods â€” the noise wraps seamlessly when coordinates advance by one period. @param x  number @param y  number @param px number  X period (tile width in noise space). @param py number  Y period (tile height in noise space). @return number  Value in [-1, 1].

**Parameters:** `x`, `y`, `px`, `py`

*Source: [src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs](src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs#L122)*

---

#### `luna.procgen.poissonDisk(w, h, min_dist, [max_attempts], [seed])`

Generates Poisson disk sample points using Bridson's algorithm.

Returns a Lua table of `{x, y}` point tables. @param w           number  Domain width. @param h           number  Domain height. @param min_dist    number  Minimum distance between any two points. @param max_attempts number (default 30) Candidates per active point. @param seed        number  (default 0) Random seed. @return table

**Parameters:** `w`, `h`, `min_dist`, `max_attempts`, `seed`

*Source: [src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs](src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs#L143)*

---

#### `luna.procgen.voronoi(w, h, pts_tbl, [opts_tbl])`

Generates a Voronoi diagram for a set of seed points.

`pts` is a Lua array of `{x, y}` tables (seed points). `opts` fields (all optional): - `warp_scale`    â€” `number`  Warp noise frequency (default 0.1). - `warp_strength` â€” `number`  Warp noise amplitude; 0 = no warp (default 0). - `seed`          â€” `number`  Seed for warp noise (default 0). Returns three flat tables of size `w * h`: - `regions`   â€” `u32` index of the closest seed point. - `dist`      â€” `f32` distance to the closest seed. - `dist2`     â€” `f32` distance to the second-closest seed. @param w    number @param h    number @param pts  table @param opts table  (optional) @return table, table, table

**Parameters:** `w`, `h`, `pts_tbl`, `opts_tbl`

*Source: [src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs](src/lua_api/procgen_api.rs#L183)*

---

## luna.scene

Registers the `luna.scene.*` scene stack, registry, data store, and depth-sorter API.

The scene stack manages a LIFO stack of Lua scene tables with optional
visual transitions. Scene tables are stored via `mlua::RegistryKey` and
identified by `SceneId`. Inter-scene data is stored similarly.

The `DepthSorter` UserData batches draw callbacks by depth for ordered
compositing each frame.

*28 entries | 28 documented*

### Functions

### DepthSorter Methods

#### `DepthSorter:add(callback, depth)`

Registers a draw callback at the given depth layer. Higher `depth` values draw in front.

@param callback : function @param depth : number

**Parameters:**

- `callback` â€” `function`: Draw callback `function()` called when flushing this layer.
- `depth` â€” `number`: Depth value determining draw order (lower = drawn first).

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L66)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:addObject(obj)`

Registers a table object with a `draw` method at the given depth.

@param obj : table

**Parameters:**

- `obj` â€” `table`: Object with a `draw()` method. Uses `obj.depth` if no explicit depth is provided.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L80)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:clear()`

Removes all registered callbacks and objects without calling them.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L130)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:flush()`

Calls all registered draw callbacks and object `draw()` methods in sorted depth order, then clears the list.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L97)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:getCount()`

Returns the number of callbacks and objects currently registered.

@return any

**Returns:** `integer` â€” number of registered draw entries.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L141)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:sort()`

Sorts all registered callbacks and objects by their depth values (ascending).

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L91)*

---


## luna.serial

Registers the `luna.serial.*` format serialization API.

Provides `luna.serial` with functions to parse and serialize JSON, TOML, and CSV
to/from Lua tables. YAML removed â€” use TOML for config (design-assumption B-05).
No file I/O â€” strings in, strings out.

## luna.spine

Registers the `luna.spine` namespace.

Provides Lua-level skeletal animation: bone hierarchies, slot bindings,
and world-transform propagation via [`Skeleton`].

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem.
Key types exported: `LuaSkeleton`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

*9 entries | 9 documented*

### Functions

### Skeleton Methods

#### `Skeleton:addBone(name, [opts])`

Adds a root bone (no parent) and returns its index.

`opts` fields (all optional): - `x`         â€” `number`  Local X offset (default 0). - `y`         â€” `number`  Local Y offset (default 0). - `rotation`  â€” `number`  Local rotation in radians (default 0). - `scale_x`   â€” `number`  Local X scale (default 1). - `scale_y`   â€” `number`  Local Y scale (default 1). @param name string @param opts table  (optional) @return number   Bone index (0-based internally, returned as Lua number).

**Parameters:** `name`, `opts`

*Source: [src/lua_api/spine_api.rs](src/lua_api/spine_api.rs#L53)*

#### `Skeleton:setPosition(x, y)`

Sets the local position of the root offset (bone 0 world position seed).

---

Propagates all local transforms down the bone hierarchy to compute

world-space positions and rotations.

## luna.terminal

Lua API bindings for the `luna.terminal.*` text-mode terminal emulator.

This binding layer uses userdata handles so terminal methods work with
idiomatic Lua colon syntax. Widget constructors return detached widget
handles that carry their own data and callbacks until `addWidget()`
attaches them to a terminal.

*55 entries | 0 documented*

### Functions
